## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillator dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves finding the acceleration (dv/dt) of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator as a function of position, velocity, and time. The acceleration is governed by restoring forces (functions of x) and possibly damping forces (functions of v), characteristic of nonlinear dynamical systems such as Duffing, Van der Pol, or driven oscillators.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Linear restoring force: dv_dt = c0 * x (simple harmonic oscillator)
- Cubic nonlinearity (Duffing): dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (Duffing oscillator restoring force)
- Linear damping + restoring: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (damped harmonic oscillator)
- Duffing with damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (damped Duffing oscillator)
- Van der Pol nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * (1 + c2 * x**2) (Van der Pol oscillator)
- Driven oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (periodically driven damped oscillator)
- Quintic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order nonlinear restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (cubic velocity damping)
- Quadratic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 (asymmetric restoring force)
- Position-velocity coupling: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 * v (nonlinear friction dependent on position)
- Softening spring with damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (driven Duffing with damping)
- Pendulum-like restoring: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) (nonlinear pendulum approximation)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (Rayleigh-type nonlinear damping)
- Mixed nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x * v**2 (energy-dependent restoring force)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x**3, x**5) ŌåÆ symmetric potential well / hardening or softening spring behavior
- Velocity-dependent terms linear in v ŌåÆ linear viscous damping or energy injection
- Products of x**2 and v ŌåÆ amplitude-dependent damping characteristic of Van der Pol-type self-excitation
- Sinusoidal functions of time ŌåÆ external periodic driving force
- Cubic position terms with opposite sign to linear term ŌåÆ Duffing-type softening/hardening spring bifurcation
- Odd powers of velocity (v**3) ŌåÆ nonlinear drag or Rayleigh-type dissipation
- Sinusoidal functions of position ŌåÆ pendulum-like large-angle nonlinearity
- Absence of explicit time dependence ŌåÆ autonomous system / conservative or self-sustained oscillator

Combining terms:

- **v term:** `(-0.333481 - 1.24947)*v = -1.582951*v`

The GT has these basis functions:

**Critical note about log(|v| + 1):** Since v takes both signs, `log(|v| + 1)` is NOT the same as `log(v┬▓ + 1)/2` or `log(v + 1)`. Let me verify: `log(|v|+1)` vs `log(v┬▓+1)`. These are different functions. For v>0: log(v+1) vs log(v┬▓+1). Not equivalent.

Also, `x*|v|^(1/3)` requires |v| since v takes both signs.

Let me now systematically check candidates:

**Candidate 1:** `c0*x + c1*v + c2*v^c3 + c4*v^c5 + c6*v^c7*x + c8*log(c9*v┬▓ + 1)`
